I'd also highly recommend the rose coffee if you want an absolutely refreshing cup of coffee with pleasant and relaxing aroma of roses combined with a calming hint of rose flavor to the end of each sip. There are delicious fresh pastries in the mornings too (they go quick though). If having incredible coffee wasn't enough the owners are two of the most genuinely nice people I've met and all of their staff are wonderful. Its a pleasure to come in enjoy a pastry, coffee, and chat to start the morning off feeling good.< /text>

< Time>
1522702151817</Time>
< Review>
As someone who is a serious chocolaholic, I'm always on the lookout for the best chocolate drinks or desserts. I think Starbuck's Mocha Frapp is pretty good, esp. if you request an additional pump (or half pump) of mocha (chocolate) And Peet's has a Mocha Javiva which can be good and isn't too coffee-strong. But then I discovered Willy's Mocha Mania. It's a sensational smoothie that uses nonfat yogurt (that I can't taste), chocolate, coffee and whatever secret ingredients it has. The manager told me that it's been around for 20 years. No surprise. I also like Willy's version of a Creamsicle (orange/vanilla smoothie) but for chocolaholics the Mocha Mania is IT. The staff are very friendly at the place, helped no doubt by my being a familiar customer with a serious Mocha Mania addiction. They're very sympathetic to that.<//Review>

<review>This place was great! My daughter has severe level 3 Autism and is extremely difficult when it comes to brushing her teeth, after repeated fails with her pediatrician trying to get a look in her mouth, we were told to go see a dentist who could offer sedation for special needs children in these type of situations. It is so cute in there and set up and decorated especially for children. My kid hates hospitals, clinics, pretty much any open white room with only scary looking medical equipment in it, she didn't even suspect a thing and was into the blocks, cartoon movie playing, and fascinated mostly with the beautiful finding Nemo themed aquarium they have built into the wall! Once we were called in, it was so different than expected , the cleanest dental place I've ever been to, not even kidding I've seen gross places that make you question sanitation .... Not this place there's more colors and toys displayed just like when you win a prize, a very smart idea,  the toys are encouraging and motivating and helps with distraction , to get the work done. My daughter was a bit fussy, but that's cuz she can't sit still being around interesting new things. Also the room is set up for multiple kids with their own cute Lil dentist chairs. We were a few seats away from another little girl getting her teeth cleaned with her family there as well. Which I think made my daughter more at ease. And she didn't feel to overwhelmed like she usually does if people in a room only focus on her. And now for the ending which was the best, my daughter actually liked the dentist lady, I'm not being dramatic when I say my kid is usually dramatic lol, but she sure made me look like a lier lol. She did pretty well, struggled a lil here and there, but she must of really liked the dentist because she gave in for once and let the dentist even brush  her upper back teeth, sorry if I sound exaggerative, but that there was amazing for me to see, it's just an autism mom thing not to many can understand :) They really know how to work with kids and make them comfortable, definitely recommended. < text>
There are a few different areas of beach along the coast that's in the city of Pacifica.. Starting at the north end of Pacifica there's Mussel Rock State Beach and trail which borders Daly City, there's the Esplanada Beach on Esplanada Ave. Than the Manor beach which has a steep trail down to the beach. Past Manor Dr right next to the SF RV Park there's a small parking lot with beach access.  Than Pacifca Pier which is next to Sharp Park Beach and a golf course. There's beach access and a great walking and if you want you can hike it up to Mori Point and enjoy a fascinating views. after that beach and over the mountains you'll have the Rockaway Beach which also has a trail up another hill headed south, than that trail you can go up and over to the other side or drive highway 1 and reach Linda Mar Beach is the official Pacifca State Beach, where most the surfers like to go, than tiny Pedro Point, Privately owned beach called Shelter Cove the lastly a trail through Shelter Cove will bring you to Gray Whale Cove State Beach.</text>

< text>
Tiny parking lot, but it has a great ocean view! There is usually a spot despite the small size, except at sunset when everyone and their mother arrives to take pictures. the beach is teeny and usually has fishermen taking the space available, although sometimes families come out to play. It is a short walk to the other side where surfers like to go. Moreover you are close to two awesome hiking trails going up to the tops of hills with even more amazing views. Finally, you can also walk around the tiny shopping area where this is a cute cash-only coffee shop and some other local treasures. Its a nice place to spend an hour or two away from the madness that occurs everywhere else.< /text>
